) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

--

--

  `id` int(9) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(191) NOT NULL,
  `handle` varchar(191) NOT NULL,
  `css` longtext NOT NULL,
  `markup` longtext NOT NULL,
  `settings` longtext
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
